Chamber of Commerce Asks for Correction of Heavy Tax on Cotton Yarn

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce sent a letter to the Consolidated Tax Bureau yesterday, stating: "Regarding the matter of directly addressing you, we received a letter on the 19th of this month from the Shanghai Association of Chaozhou Sugar and Sundry Goods Merchants, stating that our members received a telegram from Shantou stating that cotton yarn shipped to Shantou had already been subject to consolidated tax at the Shanghai Consolidated Tax Bureau upon export. However, after the goods arrived in Shantou, the Consolidated Tax Bureau wanted to collect the tax again. This double taxation is illegal and violates the clear orders of the National Government regarding unified tax rates. We have already sent a letter to the Shanghai Cotton Mill Association, requesting them to seek assistance from the Shanghai Consolidated Tax Bureau. We are now urgently requesting your Chamber to forward a message to the Shanghai Consolidated Tax Bureau to properly address the aftermath of our members' shipments to Shantou, so that the goods can be sold smoothly and avoid heavy taxes, thus maintaining commerce and friendly relations between merchants." After investigation, Article 5 of the Consolidated Tax Regulations states: "Cotton yarn and its directly woven products, as well as matches and cement, which have already been subject to consolidated tax, shall not be subject to any other taxes when transported to various provinces." According to the aforementioned situation, the Shantou Consolidated Tax Bureau is attempting to collect taxes again on goods exported from Shanghai that have already been subject to consolidated tax, which is a violation of regulations and disrupts the consolidated tax system. We are hereby requesting your office to investigate and swiftly order the Shantou Consolidated Tax Bureau to strictly correct this matter in order to uphold the tax system and maintain friendly relations. Respectfully submitted to the Consolidated Tax Bureau of the Ministry of Finance.

Miscellaneous Grain Industry Asks for Reduction of Export Tax

The Shanghai Municipal Miscellaneous Grain, Oil, and Oilcake Trade Association sent a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, stating: "Respectfully submitting this matter, we recently read in the newspaper that the revised Customs Export Tariff stipulates a tax rate of 3.4 mace for rice, an increase of 1.9 mace compared to the previous regular and additional taxes. Sesame is taxed at 4.3 mace, an increase of 2.275 mace, peanuts at 2.9 mace, an increase of 0.065 mace, broad beans and peas at 1.5 mace, an increase of 0.06 mace, and green beans and red beans at 1.8 mace, an increase of 0.09 mace. Considering that rice is related to the people's food supply, it should be allowed to circulate freely within the country, in accordance with the late Premier's instructions to regulate food supplies. The richest rice-producing provinces are Jiangsu, Anhui, Hunan, and Jiangxi, from which rice is exported and sold throughout the north and south, always requiring transshipment. Now that the export tax rate has suddenly increased, merchants will be unable to afford it, which will inevitably lead to sluggish sales. The impact of this will not only harm the people and farmers, but also impact the future of the national food supply. Therefore, the export tax should be reduced. Sesame and peanuts, as well as broad beans, peas, green beans, and red beans, are produced in Jiangsu, Anhui, Henan, and Shandong, gathered in Shanghai, and transshipped for export. They have long been needed by foreign countries, and domestic sales are limited, relying mainly on exports. If the government truly wants to support domestic productivity, it should protect and promote these exports. Therefore, the export tax should be reduced to expand national production. Since the end of the European War, commercial warfare has intensified, and almost all countries have paid attention to the progress of international trade. Therefore, they often use the power of the state to support merchants. Looking back at our country, production is lagging, commerce is declining, and most of our needs for clothing, food, housing, and transportation depend on foreign goods. The amount of wealth flowing out of the country each year is huge, amounting to hundreds of millions. Therefore, if domestic products can be exported, they should be encouraged in every way, so that merchants are willing to operate and increase the effectiveness of their foreign trade, thereby compensating for the loss of wealth to some extent. Therefore, the export tax should be reduced to encourage foreign trade. In the newly promulgated Customs Tariff, soybeans maintain the original tax rate, while soybean oil and soybean cake have been reduced. This shows that the government does not want to discourage exports. However, sesame and peanuts are both raw materials for oil production, and their properties and effects are the same. Broad beans and other similar beans are also needed by foreign countries, just like soybeans. However, the tax rates are vastly different, with light and heavy being differentiated. This is too unbalanced. Edible oil and soybean oil both belong to the oil category and should be reduced in accordance with the example of soybean oil. Therefore, the export tax should be reduced to ensure proportionality among similar products. Based on the above four points, for the purpose of circulating domestic rice, supporting farmers' economies, encouraging exports, and increasing the effectiveness of international trade, it is necessary to reduce or exempt taxes. Although the reduction of national tax revenue is minimal, the benefits to farmers and merchants are immeasurable. Therefore, we boldly submit this statement, requesting your Chamber to forward it to the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry, so that the above items can be reduced and appropriately revised in order to benefit the national economy and improve the people's livelihoods. We remain respectfully.

All Shanghai Butchers Closed Yesterday

Government Officials State That Discussions Will Resume After Business Resumes

The fresh meat industry in the city has been closed for seven days due to the slaughter tax issue. Butchers in the concessions have all stopped slaughtering starting yesterday and have gone on strike. Colleagues in Zhejiang Province have also telegraphed in response. The details of yesterday's situation are as follows:

Citywide Shutdown

Over 1,400 fresh meat shops in the Public Concession and French Concession, including Lugaoxuan, have unanimously supported the strike. After implementing the cessation of slaughter, the Suxi Slaughterhouse at Dawang Temple slaughtered all its pigs by 2 PM yesterday. The French Municipal Council Slaughterhouse at Nanyang Bridge has also ceased operations. The meat sold by concession butchers today is old meat, and they will go on strike starting tomorrow.

Municipal Government Statement

Yesterday, reporters from various newspapers visited Yu Hongjun, Secretary-General of the Municipal Government, regarding the slaughter tax case, asking for his opinion on the butchers' request to change the slaughter tax to a business tax. Yu stated that according to Article 11 of the Supplementary Measures to the Outline of Business Tax Collection in Various Provinces, the Ministry of Finance stipulates that the change from slaughter tax to business tax should be implemented in two steps. The first step is to rename the slaughter tax as a business tax, while the tax rate remains the same as the original slaughter tax rate. The second step is to change the original tax rate to the business tax rate after the business tax is ready. Regardless of whether the business tax has been implemented in this city, even if the business tax is implemented in the future, it must be implemented in stages in accordance with the outline supplement stipulated by the Ministry. Furthermore, Article 5 of the supplementary measures stipulates that the business tax should be paid directly by the taxpayer to the competent authority and must not be contracted or subcontracted by others. The government abolished the contracted donations and still collects them in accordance with the original slaughter tax rate, which is in accordance with the measures stipulated by the Ministry, and there has been no increase in the burden on citizens. The tax rate and tax amount are completely different, so there is no room for misinterpretation. The government is determined to eliminate long-standing malpractices and will only handle matters in accordance with the law. It is hoped that butchers will not be exploited by a few unscrupulous merchants and suffer losses, and it is further hoped that the public will uphold justice.

Zhejiang Merchants Respond

The Fresh Meat Industry Association received a joint telegram from the Meat Industry Associations of 16 locations in Zhejiang Province, including Jiaxing, stating: "Greetings to the Shanghai Fresh Meat Industry Association. Having read in the newspaper that your association is requesting the abolition of the heavy slaughter tax and the change to business tax, but has not received a satisfactory response, resulting in a full shutdown, we cannot help but feel deeply moved. Article 7 of the Outline for the Collection of Business Tax in Various Provinces stipulates that the slaughter tax should be abolished immediately after the establishment of the business tax. Although there are restrictions in Article 11 of the supplementary regulations, the business tax will be temporarily collected at the original tax rate as a transitional measure. However, the second step of the same regulations states that after the business tax is ready, the original tax rate will be changed to the business tax rate to achieve uniformity. Furthermore, the implementation of the business tax in Zhejiang Province has been decided and will be opened within this month, as has been announced. Since the business tax is scheduled to be opened, it is natural that the preparations have already been completed, and the old tax should be abolished and changed to the new tax. This is very clear. Your actions are to relieve the poor of heavy burdens and are worthy of being the leaders of the national meat industry. Our association expresses deep sympathy. In addition to submitting a request to the Zhejiang Provincial Government to transfer to the Ministry of Finance, requesting the abolition of the slaughter tax and the change to the business tax in accordance with the outline of the business tax in order to relieve the people's difficulties, we are also sending this telegram. We hope that you will inform the national meat industry to strive for it together, so that the effort will be halved and the goal will be easily achieved. Local areas are fortunate, and the industry is fortunate.

Jiaxing, Tongxiang, Xincheng, Chongde, Qingzhen, Wuxing, Wuzhen, Shuanglin, Lianshi, Shanlian, Qingshan, Daixi, Mayao, Deqing, Xinshi, Nanxun and other Meat Industry Associations jointly sign"

Intestine Industry Assistance

The Municipal Intestine Industry Association, because it is closely related to the meat industry, is particularly concerned. A special meeting of the Executive Committee was convened yesterday, resolving to send a letter of condolence, expressing assistance, and requesting the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to assist in resolving the issue as soon as possible.

Resolution Path

The meat industry shutdown has now been going on for seven days. Yesterday, a reporter from Xinsheng News inquired with officials and butchers about the resolution of this case. He learned that the butchers could reluctantly agree to the collection of a single layer, but the tax rate was too high to bear. They requested that the authorities understand the difficulties of the merchants and reduce the tax. The charitable undertakings previously undertaken should also be continued by the government. Officials indicated that maintaining charitable undertakings could be allowed. If the butchers agreed to the point calculation, the reduction of the tax rate could also be discussed, but the prerequisite was that business should resume first before other items could be discussed.

A Few Sand and Gravel Businesses Have Resumed Operations

Representatives Will Be Sent to Nanjing to Petition

Regarding the issue of the shutdown of the sand and gravel industry in this city, after receiving instructions from the Ministry of Finance, a small number resumed operations yesterday. The details are as follows:

Minority Resumption

After the Sand and Gravel Trade Association received instructions from the Ministry of Finance on the previous day, agreeing to revoke the tax, the association's more than 300 members resumed operations yesterday to await resolution. However, over 1,000 non-member businesses have not yet indicated that they will resume operations because the donation tax has not been completely revoked.

Petition to Nanjing

The sand and gravel industry believes that although the Ministry of Finance has instructions to investigate and revoke the tax, it is not a thorough solution. Now that they have been willing to sacrifice and stop business, they must achieve the goal completely before stopping. Therefore, it has been decided to organize a petition group to prepare a document and go to Nanjing to request the Ministry of Finance to implement the cancellation.

General Assembly Resolution

The Sand and Gravel Industry Association convened a general meeting of all members yesterday at 7 PM to discuss the matter of persuading non-members to resume business and requesting Party and government agencies to stop the collection of taxes. The resolutions are as follows: (1) Resolve to order members of the Association to persuade non-members to resume business; (2) Resolve to submit a document to Party and government agencies reporting the resumption of business; (3) Resolve to submit a document to Party and government agencies requesting the cessation of the extortionate sand and mud tax contracted by Dachang Company; (4) Resolve to send Zhou Fengzhang, Li Zefu, Lu Xiaozuo, and Chen Jianqiu to attend the meeting of the Construction Industry Association on May 23rd.

Industry Response

The Shanghai Stone Quarry, Sand, and Gravel Trade Association jointly announced to the industry yesterday, stating: "Since the implementation of the management fee for the collection of yellow sand by the Construction Department of Zhejiang Province, all our sand and gravel industry members have regarded it as the biggest obstacle to our business. At a time when taxes are being cut and reduced, there is still such a policy of exorbitant taxes. The sand and gravel industry must fight to the death to seek a line of life. However, to oppose this management fee, our colleagues should first unite and carefully plan thorough solutions, ensuring that the steps are followed properly and that the workers in the industry and the laborers of the carrying sticks and trucks do not suffer unnecessary losses. This is our humble opinion, and we trust that our colleagues will agree. We hereby inform you and respectfully request your consideration."

Party Department Meeting

The Wusong Eighth District Party Department convened a joint meeting at 2 PM on the 18th of this month for this matter, inviting various help boat households, the Sand Industry Association, and officials from the Construction Department's Sand Transport Order Office. Xu Yifei, the representative of the office, explained the process of handling the matter according to the order, and the help boat households reported on the oppression they have suffered from brokers (i.e., the Sand Industry Association) over the years. It was said that the yellow sand used for construction in Shanghai is produced in various coastal areas of Zhejiang Province. The sand has traditionally been purchased from landlords and transported to Shanghai for sale by the help boat households. However, the boat households rely on physical labor, and after their sand boats arrive in Shanghai, they are eager to return for loading and transportation in order to maintain their livelihoods, so they cannot stay in Shanghai for a long time to wait for sales. Brokers take advantage of this weakness, using their monopolistic methods to deduct tonnage and reduce prices, doing everything they can to exploit them. They also know that the boat households are short of capital, so they use a small amount of money as a tool to coerce them, preventing the boat households from selling freely forever. The boat households have suffered this oppression for many years and have been unable to find a way to eliminate it. Now that the landlords in various production areas have formed the Yitai Company to sell their own sand, they are giving the boat households preferential water feet (transportation fees) and valuing the sand by the ton so that they do not suffer losses. When the boat households heard this news, they all celebrated and transported the sand for sale. As a result, they incurred the jealousy of the brokers, who did not hesitate to use various means to disrupt the situation. On one hand, they gathered people to create disturbances under the pretext of collecting management fees, and even hired gangsters to prevent sand boats from entering the port. The boat households stated that if they did not lose anything in the water feet after paying the management fees, they would not resist in any way and would not be used by anyone to request the maintenance of the regulations. After hearing the explanations of the office representative and various help boat households, the Eighth District Party Department also expressed deep understanding. The brokers of the Sand Industry Association had nothing to say. The Eighth District Party Department has clearly understood the truth and has ignored the unreasonable demands of the Sand Industry Association.

Barge Industry News

On the 19th, the Shanghai Coal and Stone Barge Industry Association received reports from members such as Zhu Tongfu of the Xiejin Barge Transportation Company, stating that all stone boats imported from Hangzhou, Jiaxing, Huzhou, Wuxi, etc., were stopped at the docks and could not unload their goods, resulting in huge losses every day, and requested speedy relief. After receiving the report, the Association noted that coal boats were transporting as usual, supplying the needs of various transportation agencies, and there were no obstacles to uploading or unloading. They wondered why the stone boats could not unload their cargo after arriving in Shanghai. They immediately sent personnel to investigate various docks and found that the coolies on the docks were on strike, so the imported stone boats were unable to unload their cargo. In addition to requesting compensation from various brokers for all losses incurred by the boat households, the Association has informed all members.

(E) Regarding the allocation of goods sold by each factory, it was decided that Huahua Department Store and Wuzhou Soap Medicine Factory could be accommodated due to special circumstances, but no one else should use this as an example in the future. Guanghua Factory Labor Dispute Resolved

The Bureau of Social Affairs mediated a dispute involving Gu Yongjing, the manager of the silk-finishing office affiliated with the municipal dyeing industry union, and the Guanghua factory. Gu Yongjing had dismissed workers for no reason, causing resentment between labor and management, which nearly led to a strike. Yesterday, the Bureau of Social Affairs conducted a second mediation. At 1 PM, both sides were summoned for questioning. Xu Zhi, the chairman of the Second Section, attended, as well as Zhou Jinji and two others representing the labor side, and Gu Yongquan and two others representing the management side. As a result, three conditions were agreed upon: (1) The factory is willing to allow Xu Guangsheng to return to work. (2) Xu Guangsheng tore up the notice. The management will give him a demerit, taking into account the circumstances. (3) Xu Guangsheng acted improperly. He will write a letter of repentance to the factory and will work peacefully in the future. Thus, a storm was calmed.

Printing Workers' Wage Increase Movement

The wage increase movement of printing workers in this city is very tense. In recent days, over thirty factories, with more than 1,200 workers, have been asking the industry union (referring to the typesetting industry union) to promptly propose revisions to the treatment contract and increase wages. They are also voluntarily raising funds to strengthen the union's financial backing. Details of some of their demands are as follows: generally, each worker is requesting a monthly wage increase of four yuan, the employer must subsidize the workers' housing costs by four yuan per person per month, implement an eight-hour workday, and request the establishment of a school for printing workers' children. There are over twenty other demands, which are difficult to describe in detail. Over ten more factories are joining. If an accident occurs, public security will inevitably be greatly affected. It is now known that the Shanghai Typesetting Industry Union is convening meetings of cadres in various districts to discuss the direction of action in order to cope with the demands of the workers, so as to persuade and enlighten them. The general idea is to unite, wait for the union to submit a request to the higher authorities for legal action, and for workers in each factory to strictly obey discipline in order to maintain public security and not be exploited by reactionary elements,

Yarn and Cotton Market Stable. The yarn market trend is firm, with a relatively strong situation. The current yarn sales are still good, and the exchange rate has shrunk significantly. Rumors about the current situation have calmed down slightly, and American cotton has also turned to an upward trend, causing retail investors to buy in, and people are determined. A certain merchant is expected to receive a huge amount of 13,000 bales this month. The delivery items are mostly 10-count Red Lotus Bee, accounting for about 4,000 to 5,000 bales. The rest are also coarse yarns, but generally retail investors have not completely given up their plans to sell short due to the chaotic current situation, and the pressure is still heavy. There are still many who sell short when the price rises. However, judging from the overall situation, although there is no actively rising trend temporarily, it is difficult to find a sharp drop. If the Guangdong political situation does not change and the import tax is settled, there will be a large number of coarse yarn businesses, because they have not been purchased this year, and there will naturally be great hope in the future. As the exchange rate does not increase, not only can overseas goods not be shipped in, but there are exports, so in comparison, the market is quite likely to be consolidated.

Grain and Foreign Rice Sales are Slow and Prices are Falling. Yesterday's customer rice market was halted, and the market immediately became sluggish. Huilong goods opened Min Dang 100 tons in June, the price was 5 taels 5 qian 3 fen, which was 2 fen less than the previous market. Flour prices stabilized due to the weather turning stable.

Yesterday's flour market, after the opening in the morning, although the quotation of foreign wheat was good for about 2 or 3 jiao in each month's market, the inland gang's thinking was slightly relaxed because the weather had cleared, and the market saw fatigue and decline in each month because of the return of floating profits. The closing price was about 1 fen lower than the previous day. Until the opening in the afternoon, because the weather was hot and stuffy, and everyone was afraid of a downpour, the market still rose. Judging from the situation after this, it seems that there is a flood in all places because the rainfall is too sufficient. At this time, when the new wheat will come to the market, there must be clear weather to save it, otherwise it will be difficult for people to calm down. As a result, May, June and July were slightly better than before 2 li half, September was better 2 li half, and August and October were unchanged. Period Wheat's Later Market Turns Good.

Yesterday's period wheat market, after the opening in the morning, each month's market had a hovering trend. Because the weather had turned fine, the inland gang's office stomachs were slightly advanced, or they were engaged in returning goods, so the softest time was about 2 or 3 points less than the previous day. Until the opening in the afternoon, because the decline in the flour market was not much, and there were few sellers, the market's needs were still dominated by bulls, so the bids in each month were also good. Judging from this, if the pricing of foreign wheat is appropriate, it can ease people's hearts, otherwise it will be difficult to return to low prices for the time being. As a result, this month was 1 fen better than the previous day, June was 5 fen better, July was 3 fen better, August was 5 fen better, September was 3 fen better, and October was 5 fen better.

Silk and Tea Foreign Firm Silk Market Has Little Vitality. In the European and American markets, the price of Japanese silk is cheap, and the progress of Chinese silk factories is slow and stagnant. Prices have fallen sharply, especially in Shanghai factories. The market atmosphere is depressed. Yesterday, only Hexing purchased ten packages of Sichuan yellow factory silk, and Xin Shichang purchased ten packages of Bai Gan factory silk. Prices are trending down. Shaoxing High-Quality Cocoons are Scarce and Prices are Rising Sharply. Cocoon production only accounts for 30%... High-quality cocoons open at 52 yuan.

This year's early silkworms in Shaoxing's various cities and villages were frozen to death during the first sleep. During the late silkworm's major sleep, heavy rains and cold weather caused 40% to 50% of the silkworms to die of jaundice and stiff death. After being put on the wicker frames, they suffered from severe cold winds and sand. Cocoon production is very scarce. New cocoons have been listed on the market. The total harvest is only about 30%. Only 24 cocoon firms have opened scales in the entire county. The scales have been opened for three or four days, and the goods arriving on the market are few, and the cocoons are thin and of poor quality. Very few high-quality cocoons. The price of cocoons has risen sharply. The price of improved varieties of high-quality goods has risen to 52 yuan. Each firm's collection is very limited.

Qi Tea Transactions Exceed 4,000 Boxes. Yesterday's tea market in the foreign firms in this port, English firms were very interested in purchasing Qimen upper and middle grade black tea, and German and French firms also started searching and purchasing. The market turned firm. Transactions in the city for Qi tea from various routes reached 4,717 boxes. The top board still opened at 360 taels. Chinese tea merchants, in view of the shortage of production this year and the large sales in England, people's hearts turned firm again, so yesterday's market was unchanged from the previous day.

Suian Zhenmei Tea Has Arrived in Shanghai. More than 400 boxes of Zhejiang's Suian green tea have been transported from Hangzhou by Yongxinglong and Gong Shengyong tea warehouses yesterday, and samples will be available today. News from Wuyuan Tea.

Few Scales Opened. New tea from Wuyuan's various villages has been negotiated by tea houses for days. Mountain households are separated from the too harsh sale prices, which are far from covering costs, and they insist on not giving in. Except for the two places in Yintai Liujiaxia that opened scales yesterday, only one place, Chamuqiao, opened scales today. The board price is still 40 yuan, no higher or lower than yesterday's market. New tea in the Xilu Shicen, Yantian, and Huchuan areas is still being negotiated, but the sale price is only 30 yuan and has not yet been agreed upon. Judging from the stalemate between the firms and households, it seems difficult to achieve large-scale openings for a while.

Silver is Extremely Tight. In previous years, the various tea funds of this county were obtained from Yueping, Jingdezhen, and Tunxi in addition to the merchants' supply, so the silver situation was still flexible. This year, none of the tea funds of the various firms are prepared. The tea warehouses stationed in Wuyuan only lend to those who have capital and have not controlled the warehouse funds. Even the firms with tickets and capital are afraid of the danger of transporting cash from afar due to the rampant bandits. The only source of cash is the assistance of merchants in this county. However, the business of shops this year has been greatly declining, and the amount of funds released is small. Recently, the ticket price has increased from 1,370 yuan per thousand taels to 1,330 yuan, and there is still a market but no funds to exchange. The extreme tightness of silver is rare.

Mountain Households are Suffering Losses. This county has more mountains than fields, and tea production is the bulk. The livelihood of farmers throughout the year also relies on the income from tea prices. This year's tea leaves were picked early and the labor force was short, resulting in a strange shortage of harvest. According to tea households in various villages, those who produced one dan of tea in previous years only produced 40 to 50 jin of tea this year. Compared with previous years, the harvest has been reduced by 70%, 60%, 50%, and 40%. It is estimated that the total output of the county this year must be discounted by at least half. In addition, the mountain price is harsh and small, and the loss of harvest and price has left tea households wanting to cry without tears. Resignation of the Hubei Provincial Committee 6

Due to the Provincial Treasury's Deficit

(Nanjing) The entire Hubei Provincial Committee collectively resigned to the Central Government yesterday. The reason is that the province's tax revenue is insufficient. It is advocated that the city of Hankou be merged to provide financial support. Recently, He Chengjun and Liu Wendao were in Nanjing, where they reached an agreement with Chiang Kai-shek to merge the province and city, and partially reorganize the provincial government. It was internally decided that Wu Xingya would be transferred to Anhui as a Provincial Committee member and concurrently head of the Department of Civil Affairs, and Liu Wendao would be transferred to Hubei as a Provincial Committee member and concurrently head of the Department of Civil Affairs. Zhang Guanshi, a Hubei Committee member and concurrently head of the Department of Finance, was approved to resign. Upon receiving the telegram from Nanjing, the various committee members held a meeting and subsequently telegraphed Nanjing to submit their collective resignation. (Dispatch of the 21st)

(Hankou) There are widespread rumors that the provincial and municipal governments will be reorganized, with Liu Wendao and others transferred to the provincial government, and Chen Guang appointed as the head of Hankou City, under the jurisdiction of the provincial government. Liu Wendao returned to Hankou on the 20th. (Dispatch of the 21st)

He Yingqin Departs for Jiangxi Yesterday 7

(Nanjing) He Yingqin, along with his entourage and guards, departed for Jiangxi at 8:00 AM on the 21st aboard the warship "Yuzhang." Those who came to see him off included He Chengjun, He Yaozu, Chen Shaokuan, Chen Yi, and Zhou Yawei. Negotiations for the Recovery of Concessions 8

The Ministry of Foreign Affairs Prepares to Proceed

Starting with Investigation

(Nanjing) Regarding the issue of recovering concessions, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs has appointed Zhang Wohua, Deputy Chairman of the Treaty Committee, Vice Ministers Li Jinlun and Wang Jiazhen, as well as Chen Yilin and Ying Shangde, to discuss the methods. It has now been decided to start with an investigation, with a deadline of April. It will be carried out in three zones, and the special commissioners for the investigation have been designated: (1) The Yellow River Basin will be overseen by Huang Yuding, assisted by Cui Shijie. (2) The Yangtze River Basin will be overseen by Guo Shaozhen. (3) The Pearl River Basin will be overseen by Tao Shumo, assisted by Tao Lüqian. The ministry's order will be issued soon. (Dispatch of the 21st)

Organization of the Northwest Academic Exploration Group 9

(Nanjing) The Northwest Academic Exploration Group will have an annual recurring expense of 150,000 yuan. Its organization will have a Board of Directors as the highest governing body, consisting of fourteen directors. There will also be positions such as Group Leader, Deputy Group Leaders, and Group Members. The implementation plan has been drafted with an outline. The subjects of exploration are divided into five groups: Geography, Geology, Biology, Anthropology, and Archaeology. The exploration period will be four years, with the steps divided into three phases. The departure is scheduled for April of next year. (Dispatch of the 21st)

Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Board of Trustees 13

Yesterday's Meeting of the Standing Directors

(Nanjing) The Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Board of Trustees held a meeting of the standing directors at 3:00 PM on the 21st. The Chinese directors present were Zhu Jiaju, Zeng Rongfu, Wang Jiazhen, and Ye Gongchuo. The British directors present were Hoare and Brown. Zhu Jiaju chaired the meeting, which discussed various cases submitted by the second board meeting for review: (1) The rules of procedure and detailed rules of the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Board of Trustees. (2) The standard for calculating the annual interest on the Boxer Indemnity. The first case was revised according to the draft, and the second case was presented with a calculation report by accountant Zeng Rongfu. Both of the above cases were reviewed and passed by the standing directors and submitted to the third board meeting for discussion. The third board meeting is scheduled to be held in the Ministry of Railways conference hall on the morning of the 22nd. All twelve Chinese and British directors, except for Huang Hanliang, who went to Shanghai, have arrived in Nanjing and will attend on time. (Dispatch of the 21st)

(Tianjin) Zhang Xueliang's special train arrived in Tianjin at 0:30 AM on the 22nd from Pukou. Zhang is scheduled to go to Beiping on the evening of the 22nd. (Dispatch of the 21st)

Hu Ruoyu Bids Farewell to the Dutch Envoy 19

(Beiping) Hu Ruoyu hosted a banquet for the Dutch Envoy Oudenkotte this afternoon. Oudenkotte said that he has been in Beiping for more than 30 years and does not want to leave this second hometown. It is not yet decided whether he will be able to return to Beiping. He hopes that the people of China and the Netherlands will become increasingly friendly. Qi Dapeng hosted a banquet for the Dutch Envoy in the evening. (Dispatch of the 21st)

Inner Mongolian Princes' Conference 20

Convened by the League Leader of Zhangyuan

(Beiping) The Ude area of Inner Mongolia is frequently invaded by Outer Mongolian Red Bandits. The League Leader of Zhangyuan Sansixing League has initiated a conference of Inner Mongolian Princes to discuss joint defense and village clearing measures. It is reported that the princes who are staying in Beiping and Tianjin have been notified to go to Chahar for the meeting. (Dispatch of the 21st)

Business Circles in Beiping and Tianjin Oppose Production and Sales Tax 21

(Beiping) The Hebei Special Production and Sales Tax is being levied today. Beiping City has not yet collected it due to incomplete preparations. The Chamber of Commerce held a general meeting of representatives from various industries today, with more than 100 people in attendance. They unanimously resolved to oppose the Production and Sales Tax and immediately submitted a document to Deputy Commander Zhang, the Northeast Political Committee, and the Ministry of Finance, requesting that it not be implemented. (Dispatch of the 21st)

(Beiping) Xiong Lie, the Director of the Beiping District Production and Sales Tax Bureau, took office this morning. (Dispatch of the 21st)

(Beiping) Because of their opposition to the Production and Sales Tax, the Beiping Chamber of Commerce sent representatives Sun Kuifu, Qi Huating, and others to Tianjin tonight to petition Zhang. Today, Fushengxiang had a large batch of furs seized in Fengtai. The merchants gathered and decided that if any goods were seized, they would all be abandoned and no tax would be paid. The losses would be borne jointly by the firms. (Dispatch of the 21st)

(Tianjin) The Hebei Province Special Tax Goods Production and Sales Tax was levied on the 21st. The City Chamber of Commerce and various trade associations sent more than 20 representatives to the City Party Headquarters on the morning of the 21st to petition, saying that the Production and Sales Tax does not exist in other provinces and is only being implemented in Hebei Province. If it is not abolished, the merchants will have to close their businesses. The Party Headquarters agreed to convey this to the officials. (Dispatch of the 21st)

Kailuan Coal Mine Dispute 22

Labor-Management Mediation in Progress

Qian Chengxu Mediates Coal Transportation Matters

(Tianjin) The Kailuan Labor-Management Mediation Committee held its first meeting in the Department of Industry on the morning of the 21st. The labor representatives present were Zhang Yutang and Ni Changsheng. The management representatives present were Zhao Junda and Bo Lanting. The Department of Industry representatives were Xi Zhanmei and Guo Shaoyi. The Tangshan Public Security Bureau representative was Lu Heng. Chairman Ding reported on the process of moving the mediation to Tianjin. The labor side argued that the work stoppage should be lifted first, and then other matters should be discussed. The management side argued that transportation should be restored first, and then the lifting of the work stoppage would not be a problem. The two sides argued fiercely. After Ding explained that the committee should only discuss labor-management disputes and not labor-management conflicts, the labor side still insisted that lifting the work stoppage was a prerequisite, and the management side insisted that restoring coal transportation on the Beining Railway was a prerequisite. Finally, Ding agreed to conduct negotiations outside the meeting, and the two sides remained silent. The discussion of wage increase conditions continued, but there were no concrete results. The meeting will continue on the 22nd. The scheduled meeting period is five days, but it may need to be extended by several days. (Dispatch of the 21st)

(Tianjin) Qian Chengxu, a representative of the National Federation of Commerce and the China General Labor Union, came to Tianjin to mediate the coal transportation issue between Kailuan and Beining. He proposed methods for coal transportation and guaranteeing the performance of liquidation procedures to both the railway and the mine. After days of contact, both sides expressed that they would consider it and may accept the mediation method soon. The mine side sent Chen Tingjun as a special commissioner responsible for negotiations. Qian is scheduled to go to Beiping on the 22nd to visit the Western Hills. (Dispatch of the 21st)

Gong Bingfan Attacks Donggu 23

Xu's Troops Pressing Towards Ningdu

(Nanjing) A Jiangxi telegram reports that Gong Bingfan led his troops to attack Donggu, with fierce fighting for three days and nights. He himself arrived in Ji'an on the 20th. Furthermore, Feng Yuwai, Deputy Commander of the 9th Army, led all of the 47th Regiment to reinforce the Gong Bingfan division attacking the Red bandits in Donggu on the 17th. The troops engaged in fierce fighting with the bandits all day. A certain regiment of the division broke into the bandits' den, killing many enemies. They are currently in a stalemate. (Dispatch of the 21st)

(Hankou) Military news reports that the Jiangxi bandits are now only entrenched in the Ruijin, Shicheng, and Xingguo areas. Xu's troops have crossed Guangchang and are pressing towards Ningdu. Mao's troops are following up, and Sun Lianzhong has also reached the Ningdu border from Xiaotian, preparing for a general offensive. (Dispatch of the 21st)

(Hankou) He Yingqin, in order to eliminate the remnants of the Wan Tong bandits, has ordered that all areas north of the Yuan River be under the command of Xu Yuanquan, who will immediately begin the suppression. (Dispatch of the 21st)

Shanxi Province's Administrative Guidelines 24

(Taiyuan) Shang Zhen told reporters that the difficulties in Shanxi have been overcome. In the future, the administrative guidelines will change from passive to active: (1) Rectifying officialdom and establishing training schools for county magistrates and district chiefs, summoning the county magistrates and district chiefs to return for strict training. (2) Rectifying finance. The central government has agreed to restore financial bonds, and the Department of Finance is currently drafting a plan to send personnel to Nanjing to request instructions within days. After the bonds are determined, the provincial currency will be reorganized to stabilize public sentiment. (3) Strictly enforcing the ban on opium. The regulations on punishing the manufacture and sale of opium dross have been passed and will be implemented seriously in order to restore social vitality. (4) Reforming education, striving for innovation, and establishing a foundation for social talent. (Dispatch of the 21st)

Anti-Bandit Troops in Southern Shandong Return to Defense 25

(Jinan) Han, considering that the bandits in Baodugou have been eliminated, ordered the various troops to return to their defenses. Gu Liangmin's 22nd Division's directly subordinate troops returned to Jinan. Tang Yaoxun's two regiments are stationed in Qufu, and one regiment is transferred to Sishui. Chen Yaohan's division has one regiment stationed in Feixian to suppress the Mengshan bandits. (21st)

(Jinan) Liu Shuxiang, Chief of the General Headquarters Staff Office, along with the various departments, and Gu Liangmin, Commander of the 22nd Division, along with the various departments and the Special Service Battalion, returned to Jinan from Tengxian today. (Dispatch of the 21st)

He's Bandits Flee to Gucheng 26

(Hankou) Military news reports that the remnants of He's bandits fled from Fangxian to Gucheng and attempted to use Xieshan as a base. The Gucheng County Magistrate has telegraphed the province to report. (Dispatch of the 21st)

(Hankou) Military news reports that He's bandits fled to Gucheng and became unmanageable, fleeing to Zhushaping, Mingyangdong, and the Balichuan area. Li Guizhong was ordered to pursue and suppress them, and the Baokang County Magistrate also mobilized the militia to block them. (Dispatch of the 21st)

(Hankou) Military news reports that Wang's regiment of Xia Douyin's division occupied Hailongshan in Macheng yesterday, killing many bandits. Dai Minquan's division defeated Red bandits in Maboling and other places, pursuing them to Lingxi. Li Yunheng sent Zheng Yuncang to Hankou on the 20th, who will transfer to Hunan. (Dispatch of the 21st)

(Hankou) Zeng Yiding will immediately lead various warships to patrol the Yangtze River and protect merchants and travelers. (Dispatch of the 21st)

Chen Guang's Troops Conduct Suppression Operations Against Remnant Bandits in Pingjiang and Liuyang 27

Bandit Forces Roaming Near Liuhu

(Changsha) According to reports, the two bandit forces of Kong Hechong and Xu Hong, who had been causing disturbances in the northern townships of Liuyang, were severely suppressed by Chen Guang's troops of our New 32nd Division. One part fled to eastern Liuyang, and the other part fled to Baogaidong. On the 17th, remnant bandits, about two or three hundred with over a hundred guns, again fled to Nankeng and Shangping. Chen's troops went to suppress them and achieved many gains. The remnant bandits fled towards the Shiyanguan Mountain area. Bai Shinuo, the Liuyang County Magistrate and concurrently commander of the Security Regiment, departed for the northern townships on the 18th to suppress the remnant bandits. (Dispatch of the 20th)

(Changsha) Liu Jianxu, concurrently Director of the Pingjiang-Liuyang Pacification Office, decided to return to Pingjiang within days to preside over the suppression because the Red bandits in Pingjiang and Liuyang have not been completely eliminated. (Dispatch of the 20th)

(Changsha) According to reports, the guerrilla teams of the Chaling Red bandits who had been causing disturbances in various parts of Ling County were severely attacked by Zhang Kongyi's regiment of our New 31st Division and have fled to Suichuan on the Jiangxi border. The suppression of the remnant bandits is currently underway in order to pacify the area. (Dispatch of the 20th)

(Changsha) According to reports, a part of the Pseudo 7th Army, about two thousand strong with about a thousand guns, have been causing disturbances in various parts of Pingxiang. They have suffered heavy losses after repeated suppression by our army and have fled in disarray to various deep mountains in the Wanzai area. Furthermore, scattered Red bandit units have suddenly occupied Cihua, Huangmao, Tongmu, and other places, frequently launching attacks and disturbances, hoping to unite and harm the area. Wang Yuying's brigade of our New 31st Division is currently joining forces with Zhu Yaohua's brigade to attack the bandits from both sides. (Dispatch of the 20th)

(Changsha) Zhang Ying, Commander of the New 11th Division, telegraphed the province on the 18th, stating briefly, "According to reports, Ma Kunshan's brigade is suppressing the remnant bandits near Hongshui Harbor, and Peng's division and Hu's regiment are cooperating to attack them from both sides. They engaged in fierce fighting with the bandits near Liuhu for a long time. The bandit troops suffered more than a hundred casualties and fled in a state of disarray. Our army is currently suppressing them in the Tuanzhou area." (Dispatch of the 20th)

Changsha Commemoration of the Anti-Communist Campaign 28

Hunanese in Beijing Also Hold a Commemorative Meeting

(Changsha) All circles held a commemorative meeting for the fourth anniversary of the Anti-Communist Campaign on the 21st, with more than ten thousand people in attendance. Zhang Kailian and others delivered speeches, hoping to continue to eliminate reactionary warlords and complete the anti-communist work. A telegram was passed on the spot to Chen Jitang, urging him to maintain peace and complete the anti-communist campaign. All newspapers were suspended. (Dispatch of the 21st)

(Nanjing) The Hunanese Association in Beijing held a commemorative meeting for the fourth anniversary of the Anti-Communist Campaign today. Jiang Yuhuan presided over the meeting and reported. Representatives Xu Ke Xiang, Luo Shuren, Luo Jiefu, and Lulushan all gave reports on the process of the Anti-Communist Campaign. (Dispatch of the 21st)

Guangdong Provincial Government to be Reorganized on June 1 29

(Hong Kong) News says that the Guangdong Provincial Government will be reorganized on June 1, with one Chairman and the number of committee members increased to nine. A Department of Industry and a Bureau of Foreign Affairs will be added. (Dispatch of the 21st)

(Hong Kong) On the evening of the 21st, Ye Qi, Feng Zhuwan, and others arrived in Hong Kong by special train. (Dispatch of the 21st)

(Hong Kong) Tang Shaoyi is scheduled to go to the province on the 22nd. (Dispatch of the 21st)

Bandit Alarm in the Countryside of Suzhou 30

Shiqiaotou and Yaojiabang Attacked and Looted by Bandits

(Suzhou) At about 9:00 PM on the 20th, a large group of bandits arrived in the villages of Shiqiaotou and Yaojiabang, on the border of Suzhou and Changshu, and looted every household. Before leaving, they also kidnapped five hostages and killed three villagers. Yesterday morning, the bandits fled to the Lucun Wangchuantou area of Suzhou and also carried out large-scale searches, looting, and kidnapping of two people, fleeing towards Yangcheng Lake. (Dispatch of the 21st)

Unit of the New Export Tariff 31

(Nanjing) The unit of the new export tariff is the yuan, which does not apply to the Customs Tael system. However, whether it applies to the gold standard is to be declared later. At the same time, whether there are any difficulties due to the appreciation and depreciation of the gold standard and the yuan system is also to be studied. The Ministry of Finance is now ordering the Inspector General of Customs to promptly draft and submit a report for review and approval. (Dispatch of the 20th)

Results of the Survey of the Yangtze River Waterway 32

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Communications, considering the changes in the Yangtze River estuary and waterway, dispatched Song Xishang, Director of the Engineering Department of the Yangtze River Waterway Improvement Committee, to conduct a field survey in conjunction with commissioners dispatched by the Construction Committee and the Department of Navy. They believe that the entire plan, from Jiangyin to below the estuary, should be started from the Nantong area. The committee's survey team is scheduled to move to the lower reaches for surveying starting in July. The required construction costs will be supplemented by the sandy fields reclaimed below Jiangyin, after consultation with the Ministry of Finance. (Dispatch of the 21st)

Military Advisory Council to be Established at the End of the Month 33

(Nanjing) The Military Advisory Council is scheduled to be formally established at the end of this month. Military Research Association and Political Research Association will also be formed, with the counselors and advisors taking their respective positions, specializing in military and political research for consultation. The candidates for counselors and advisors will be decided within days and announced by decree. (Dispatch of the 21st)

Medical Officers of All Railways Must Verify Diplomas 34

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Railways believes that the medical personnel of the various railways are directly related to the lives and health of the employees, and those who have not graduated from specialized schools or above will definitely be unqualified. Therefore, it has issued an order to all railways that, in the future, the appointment of medical personnel must be presented with a diploma for verification in order to prevent opportunism. (Dispatch of the 21st)

Results of the Beijing Municipal Higher Examination Announced 35

(Nanjing) One hundred and ninety people registered for the Beijing Municipal Higher Examination. The groups were held on the 14th, 15th, and 16th. One hundred and seventy-one people actually took the exam. After the exam was completed, the Committee of Classical Examinations assessed the results as A and B, and announced them on the 21st. A total of seven people passed all subjects, and one hundred and forty people passed by subject. (Dispatch of the 21st)

Tibetan, Kang, and Qinghai Representatives Host a Banquet for the Panchen Lama 36

(Nanjing) More than a hundred representatives from Tibet, Xikang, and Qinghai in Beijing hosted a banquet for the Panchen Lama at the Shuxia Restaurant on the afternoon of the 21st and took a photo as a souvenir. (Dispatch of the 21st)

Ministry of Military Affairs Strictly Prohibits the Abuse of Torture 37

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Military Affairs believes that the military and police agencies in various provinces and regions handling bandit cases often abuse various forms of torture. Those interrogated, unable to bear the pain, often confess falsely, resulting in unjust cases. Before their guilt has been determined, they have already suffered the punishment for the crime. If they have been falsely implicated or due to a misunderstanding, even if they can be exonerated later, their bodies have already been damaged, which is a violation of humanity. Therefore, it is strictly ordering its subordinates to strictly prohibit this. (Dispatch of the 21st)
